	<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">Great Britain at the 1920 Summer Olympics</h1>

<p><b><a href="/wiki/Great_Britain_at_the_Olympics" title="Great Britain at the Olympics">Great Britain</a></b>, represented by the <a href="/wiki/British_Olympic_Association" title="British Olympic Association">British Olympic Association</a> (BOA), competed at the <b><a href="/wiki/1920_Summer_Olympics" title="1920 Summer Olympics">1920 Summer Olympics</a></b> in <a href="/wiki/Antwerp" title="Antwerp">Antwerp</a>, <a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgium</a>. 234 competitors, 218 men and 16 women, took part in 84 events in 21 sports.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sports-reference_1-0"><a href="#cite_note-sports-reference-1">[1]</a></sup> British athletes won fifteen gold medals (up from ten in 1912) and 43 medals overall, finishing third, something they did not do again until <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/London_2012" title="London 2012">London 2012</a>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Aquatics">Aquatics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Great_Britain_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Aquatics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Diving">Diving</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Great_Britain_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Diving">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Diving_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics" title="Diving at the 1920 Summer Olympics">Diving at the 1920 Summer Olympics</a></div>
<p>Five divers, three men and two women, represented Great Britain in 1920. It was the nation's third appearance in the sport. Just as in 1912, the women had the better showing for the country. Armstrong posted the country's best result to that point, taking the silver medal in the platform. White, who had won Great Britain's only previous medal in the sport, was unable to match her bronze from 1912 and took fourth place in the platform.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Swimming">Swimming</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Great_Britain_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Swimming">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Swimming_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics" title="Swimming at the 1920 Summer Olympics">Swimming at the 1920 Summer Olympics</a></div>
<p>Eighteen swimmers, twelve men and six women, represented Great Britain in 1920. It was the nation's fourth appearance in the sport. Great Britain won two medals, one in each of the relays. The men took bronze, while the women took silver. Jeans was the only individual finalist for the country, advancing to the finals in both of the women's events and taking fourth place each time.
</p><p><small><i>Ranks given are within the heat.</i></small>
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Water_polo">Water polo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Great_Britain_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Water polo">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Water_polo_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics" title="Water polo at the 1920 Summer Olympics">Water polo at the 1920 Summer Olympics</a></div>
<p>Great Britain competed in the Olympic water polo tournament for the fourth time in 1920, the fifth appearance of the sport in the Olympics. Britain won its fourth (and final, through 2008) gold medal in the sport.
</p><p>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bergvall_System" title="Bergvall System">Bergvall System</a> was used in 1920. Great Britain won all three of its matches, taking the gold medal.
</p>

<dl><dt>Final rank</dt>
<dd><span data-sort-value="01 !"><img alt="1st, gold medalist(s)" data-file-height="16" data-file-width="16" decoding="async" height="16" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/47/Gold_medal_icon.svg/16px-Gold_medal_icon.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/47/Gold_medal_icon.svg/24px-Gold_medal_icon.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/47/Gold_medal_icon.svg/32px-Gold_medal_icon.svg.png 2x" width="16"/></span> Gold</dd></dl>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Athletics">Athletics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Great_Britain_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Athletics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Athletics_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics" title="Athletics at the 1920 Summer Olympics">Athletics at the 1920 Summer Olympics</a></div>
<p>41 athletes represented Great Britain in 1920. It was the nation's sixth appearance in athletics, having competed in the sport at every Olympics. With four medals of each type, Great Britain was the third most successful nation in athletics, behind the United States and Finland.
</p><p><small><i>Ranks given are within the heat.</i></small>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Boxing">Boxing</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Great_Britain_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Boxing">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Boxing_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics" title="Boxing at the 1920 Summer Olympics">Boxing at the 1920 Summer Olympics</a></div>
<p>16 boxers represented Great Britain at the 1920 Games. It was the nation's second appearance in boxing. Great Britain was one of two countries to send two boxers in each of the eight weight classes, along with the United States. The British boxers won a total of six medals, one more than Canada and two more than the United States, but fell behind the Americans in number of gold medals three to two.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Cycling">Cycling</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Great_Britain_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Cycling">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Cycling_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics" title="Cycling at the 1920 Summer Olympics">Cycling at the 1920 Summer Olympics</a></div>
<p>Thirteen cyclists represented Great Britain in 1920. It was the nation's fourth appearance in the sport. Great Britain was one of six different nations to win a gold medal in the six cycling events; the British team also took three silvers and one bronze to make the nation the most successful cycling team in 1920. All of Great Britain's medals came in track cycling, with the gold coming from Lance and Ryan's tandem.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Fencing">Fencing</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Great_Britain_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Fencing">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Fencing_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics" title="Fencing at the 1920 Summer Olympics">Fencing at the 1920 Summer Olympics</a></div>
<p>Eighteen fencers represented Great Britain in 1920. It was the nation's fourth appearance in the sport. The British team's best individual result came from its only event finalist, Dalglish, who placed eighth in the sabre. The foil team placed fifth for the best overall result for Britain.
</p><p><small><i>Ranks given are within the group.</i></small>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Field_hockey">Field hockey</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Great_Britain_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Field hockey">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Field_hockey_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics" title="Field hockey at the 1920 Summer Olympics">Field hockey at the 1920 Summer Olympics</a></div>
<p>Great Britain competed in field hockey for the second time, fielding a single team this time. The team took the gold medal in the four-team round robin, defeating each of the other three teams.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Football">Football</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Great_Britain_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Football">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Football_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics" title="Football at the 1920 Summer Olympics">Football at the 1920 Summer Olympics</a></div>
<p>Great Britain competed in the Olympic football tournament for the fourth time, having missed only the 1904 tournament. The country had won gold medals in each of its first three appearances while going undefeated. The team's streak was abruptly halted in 1920, however, with a stunning first round loss to Norway.
</p>
<dl><dt>First round</dt></dl>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Gymnastics">Gymnastics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Great_Britain_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Gymnastics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Gymnastics_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics" title="Gymnastics at the 1920 Summer Olympics">Gymnastics at the 1920 Summer Olympics</a></div>
<p>Twenty-seven gymnasts represented Great Britain in 1920. It was the nation's fifth appearance in the sport, matched only by France. The British squad included only one team, with no gymnasts competing in the individual all-around. The team came in last place of the five competing countries.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Artistic_gymnastics">Artistic gymnastics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Great_Britain_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Artistic gymnastics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Modern_pentathlon">Modern pentathlon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Great_Britain_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Modern pentathlon">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Modern_pentathlon_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics" title="Modern pentathlon at the 1920 Summer Olympics">Modern pentathlon at the 1920 Summer Olympics</a></div>
<p>Four pentathletes represented Great Britain in 1920. It was the nation's second appearance in the sport, having competed in both instances of the Olympic pentathlon.
</p><p><small><i>A point-for-place system was used, with the lowest total score winning.</i></small>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Polo">Polo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Great_Britain_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Polo">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Polo_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics" title="Polo at the 1920 Summer Olympics">Polo at the 1920 Summer Olympics</a></div>
<p>Great Britain competed in the Olympic polo tournament for the third time, the only nation to have competed in each edition of the competition to that point (and, eventually, the entire time polo was played at the Olympics). Great Britain fielded a single team in 1920, as opposed to 1900 and 1908, when the country had players on six of the eight teams to play. The British team nevertheless took another gold medal, defeating Belgium in the semifinals and Spain in the final.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Rowing">Rowing</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Great_Britain_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Rowing">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Rowing_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics" title="Rowing at the 1920 Summer Olympics">Rowing at the 1920 Summer Olympics</a></div>
<p>Ten rowers represented Great Britain in 1920. It was the nation's fourth appearance in the sport. Both of the British boats earned silver medals; in each instance, it was an American boat which beat Great Britain's representative in the final.
</p><p><small><i>Ranks given are within the heat.</i></small>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sailing">Sailing</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Great_Britain_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Sailing">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Sailing_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics" title="Sailing at the 1920 Summer Olympics">Sailing at the 1920 Summer Olympics</a></div>
<p>Six sailors represented Great Britain in 1920. It was the nation's third appearance in the sport. Britain had the only female sailor of 1920. Both of the nation's boats took gold medals, without competition in the 18 foot class and over a Norwegian team in the 7 metre.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Skating">Skating</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Great_Britain_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Skating">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Figure_skating">Figure skating</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Great_Britain_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Figure skating">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Figure_skating_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics" title="Figure skating at the 1920 Summer Olympics">Figure skating at the 1920 Summer Olympics</a></div>
<p>Six figure skaters represented Great Britain in 1920. It was the nation's second appearance in the sport; Great Britain was one of three countries to compete in both Summer Olympics figure skating competitions. The British team was able to capture only a single bronze medal in 1920.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Shooting">Shooting</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Great_Britain_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Shooting">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Shooting_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics" title="Shooting at the 1920 Summer Olympics">Shooting at the 1920 Summer Olympics</a></div>
<p>Seven shooters represented Great Britain in 1920. It was the nation's fifth appearance in the sport; France was one of three nations (along with Denmark and France) to have competed at each Olympic shooting contest to that point. The British shooters were unable to secure a medal for the first time since 1900.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Tennis">Tennis</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Great_Britain_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Tennis">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Tennis_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics" title="Tennis at the 1920 Summer Olympics">Tennis at the 1920 Summer Olympics</a></div>
<p>Eight tennis players, four men and four women, competed for Great Britain in 1920. It was the nation's fifth appearance in the sport, tied with France for the most of any country. The doubles competitions were Great Britain's strength, with both gold medals coming from pairs—men's and women's. The country added a pair of silver medals in the women's and mixed doubles. The British players also took a pair of medals in the women's singles; Holman took silver and McKane won the bronze.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Tug_of_war">Tug of war</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Great_Britain_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Tug of war">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Tug_of_war_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics" title="Tug of war at the 1920 Summer Olympics">Tug of war at the 1920 Summer Olympics</a></div>
<p>Great Britain competed in the Olympic tug of war tournament for the third time in 1920, the final appearance of the sport in the Olympics. Along with Sweden and the United States, Great Britain's three appearances in the five Olympic tug of war tournaments were the most of any nation.
</p><p>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bergvall_System" title="Bergvall System">Bergvall System</a> was used in 1920. Great Britain won all three of its matches, taking the gold medal to become the only country to win two Olympic golds in the tug of war.
</p><p>All matches were best-of-three pulls.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Weightlifting">Weightlifting</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Great_Britain_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Weightlifting">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Weightlifting_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics" title="Weightlifting at the 1920 Summer Olympics">Weightlifting at the 1920 Summer Olympics</a></div>
<p>Two weightlifters represented Great Britain in 1920. It was the nation's second appearance in the sport, having competed in 1896 but not 1900.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Wrestling">Wrestling</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Great_Britain_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Wrestling">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Wrestling_at_the_1920_Summer_Olympics" title="Wrestling at the 1920 Summer Olympics">Wrestling at the 1920 Summer Olympics</a></div>
<p>Ten wrestlers competed for Great Britain in 1920. It was the nation's fourth appearance in the sport. The British wrestlers competed only in the freestyle, with two wrestlers in each weight class. Bernard and Wright took bronze medals; they were the only two Britons to get any wins at all, winning two matches apiece.
</p>
